    <li> I was given this by a blogger friend to test and give a review for her blog.  (BTW - great way to try out new products without having to buy them!)  Hyaluronic Acid will plump up the top layers of your skin for immediate results, but know that it does not make a long term difference - you have to keep using it to get those results.  Vitamin C is a little different, it is a building block for healthy skin and connective tissue and it will help in the longer term.  HOWEVER.  No matter what any company says, Vitamin C is not stable and it should be refrigerated.  So many companies making these products say to store at room temperature, but not true.  Keep it in the fridge, you will get better results.  The jury is out as to how well topical Vitamin C is absorbed by the skin, but if you get nice results (I did!) then the skin can absorb at least enough to make a difference.    Tips:  More is not necessarily better.  I tried it two ways - putting a lot on in the morning, once a day, and then less morning and night, twice a day.  The twice a day did better, and the once a day using a lot left my skin a tad sticky.  My recommendation is apply a few drops at a time until you cover face, neck, etc. that you want to treat.  Another tip: I also use it on my hands.  I am starting to get discoloration spots on my hands, and this has helped lessen them.    When I test products for my blogger friend, I first try the product all by itself to see what results it gives alone. I can say that this product gave decent results.  I then use products with my regular routine and see how it works together.  That&#x27;s when I saw amazing results. The Bel Essence alone gave me great results, the Vitamin C Serum gave me good results, but the two together are really powerful.    Note:  It takes a minute for the Vitamin C to be absorbed in your skin, and the oil also takes a minute to absorb.
